Ms.&#160;Mukherjee is currently Chairwoman and Chief Executive Officer of Pernod Ricard NA. The Board has not yet determined to which committees it will appoint Ms.&#160;Mukherjee. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ms.&#160;Mukherjee will receive the same compensation and indemnification as our other <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-employee</span> directors. The form of indemnification agreement is an exhibit to our Annual Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> filed with the SEC on February&#160;4, 2022. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">There are no transactions between Ms.&#160;Mukherjee and us that would be reportable under Item 404(a) of Regulation <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-K.</span> Ms.&#160;Mukherjee was not selected pursuant to any arrangement or understanding between her and any other person. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A copy of our press release regarding these events is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Appoints Ann Mukherjee to Board of Directors </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>CHICAGO, December</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;13, 2022</B> &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) today announced the appointment
of Ann Mukherjee, Chairwoman and Chief Executive Officer of Pernod Ricard North America, to the Company&#146;s Board of Directors, effective January&nbsp;1, 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We welcome Ann to our Board and look forward to benefitting from her strong track record in leading and advising multinational consumer
packaged goods companies,&#148; said Dirk Van de Put, Chairman&nbsp;&amp; CEO of Mondel&#275;z International. &#147;Her expertise in consumer insights, commercial execution and brand innovation will provide important perspective to our Board and
team as we continue advancing our Vision 2030 strategy as a global snacking leader.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mukherjee has served as Chairwoman and Chief
Executive Officer of Pernod Ricard North America, a global leader in wine and spirits, since December 2019. Previously, she served as Global Chief Commercial Officer and Global Chief Marketing Officer for S.C. Johnson&nbsp;&amp; Son, Inc., a
multinational consumer product manufacturer. Earlier, she held several senior positions with PepsiCo, Inc., a multinational food and beverage corporation, including President, Global Snacks Group and Global Insights, as well as Senior Vice President
and Chief Marketing Officer, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Frito-Lay,</FONT> Inc., a subsidiary of PepsiCo. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mukherjee&#146;s
appointment expands the size of the Company&#146;s Board of Directors to 11 members. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2021 net revenues
of approximately $29&nbsp;billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>OREO</I>, <I>belVita </I>and <I>LU </I>biscuits; <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk</I>, <I>Milka </I>and <I>Toblerone </I>chocolate; <I>Sour
Patch Kids </I>candy and <I>Trident </I>gum. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit www.mondelezinternational.com or follow the company on Twitter at
www.twitter.com/MDLZ. </P>
</DIV></Center>
